<div class=\"item-list\">    <div class=\"view-list\">\n  <ul>          <li class=\"view-list-item views-row views-row-1 views-row-odd views-row-first views-row-last\">  \n          <div class=\"field-content\"><div class=\"post-block\">\n\n      <div class=\"post-image\">\n            <a><img src=\"http://obiectivbr.ro/sites/default/files/editorial_0.jpg\" alt=\"editorial\" class=\"post-meta-user\">\n<i class=\"fa fa-user\"></i> Mircea DOAGĂ\n</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"post-created\">\n\t\t\t\tApr 21, 2017 \n\t\t\t</div>\n\t       </div>\n               <div
